\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Fortran API functions for MMG3D library. 

\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Author}
Algiane Froehly (Inria/\+UBordeaux) 
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxyVersion}{Version}
5 
\end{DoxyVersion}
\begin{DoxyDate}{Date}
01 2014 
\end{DoxyDate}
\begin{DoxyCopyright}{Copyright}
GNU Lesser General Public License. 
\end{DoxyCopyright}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Use the MMG3\+D\+\_\+ prefix\+: MMG5\+\_\+ prefix will became obsolete soon... 
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Please, refer to the \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmg3d_8h}{mmg3d/libmmg3d.\+h}} file for functions documentation.
\end{DoxyNote}
Define the Fortran API functions for MMG3D library\+: adds function definitions with upcase, underscore and double underscore to match any fortran compiler. 

Definition in file \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functionsf__3d_8c_source}{API\+\_\+functionsf\+\_\+3d.\+c}}.
